-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `Administrador`
--

CREATE TABLE `Administrador` (
  `IdAdministrador` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `nombre` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `telefono` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `mail` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `tipo` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `login` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `hashPass` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `tokenReset` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `fechaHoraReset` datetime NOT NULL,
  `fechaUltimoAcceso` datetime NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

--

CREATE TABLE `Empresa` (
  `IdEmpresa` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `IdPersona` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `nombre` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `mail` varchar(200) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `cif` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `login` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `hashPass` varchar(256) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `tokenReset` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `fechaHoraReset` datetime NOT NULL,
  `arrayIdPersona` varchar(8000) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `observaciones` text CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `fechaUltimoAcceso` datetime DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `Reclamacion`
--

CREATE TABLE `Reclamacion` (
  `IdReclamacion` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `IdPersona` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `fechaHora` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `texto` text,
  `respuesta` text,
  `estado` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `Registro`
--

CREATE TABLE `Registro` (
  `IdRegistro` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `fechaHora` datetime NOT NULL,
  `tipo` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `contenido` mediumtext CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

  `fechaFinContrato` date DEFAULT NULL,

  `hijosMenores25` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `usuario` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `hashpass` varchar(500) NOT NULL,
  `activo` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura para la vista `vista_eventos`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vista_eventos`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `vista_eventos`  AS SELECT `e`.`IdEvento` AS `IdEvento`, `e`.`IdPersona` AS `IdPersona`, `e`.`IdClientePersona` AS `IdClientePersona`, `e`.`titulo` AS `titulo`, `e`.`fechaHoraInicio` AS `fechaHoraInicio`, `e`.`fechaHoraFin` AS `fechaHoraFin`, `e`.`descripcion` AS `descripcion`, `e`.`notificar` AS `notificar`, `e`.`notificacionEnviada` AS `notificacionEnviada`, if((timestampdiff(DAY,now(),`e`.`fechaHoraInicio`) <= 2),1,0) AS `paraEnviar`, if(isnull(`e`.`IdClientePersona`),convert(`p`.`mail` using utf8mb4),`cp`.`mail`) AS `mailNotificacion`, `p`.`nombre` AS `nombrePersona`, `cp`.`nombre` AS `nombreCliente`, `p`.`mail` AS `mailPersona` FROM ((`evento` `e` left join `clientepersona` `cp` on((`e`.`IdClientePersona` = `cp`.`IdClientePersona`))) left join `persona` `p` on((`e`.`IdPersona` = `p`.`IdPersona`)))  ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura para la vista `vista_expediente`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vista_expediente`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `vista_expediente`  AS SELECT `e`.`IdExpediente` AS `IdExpediente`, `e`.`IdPersona` AS `IdPersona`, concat('Id.Cliente: -',`c`.`IdPersona`,'- <br/>',`c`.`nombre`) AS `v_datosCliente`, `e`.`asunto` AS `asunto`, `e`.`juzgado` AS `juzgado`, concat('Nº:',`e`.`numeroProcedimiento`,'<br/>',`e`.`procedimiento`) AS `v_datosProcedimiento`, `e`.`estado` AS `estado`, `g`.`nombre` AS `v_datosGestor`, concat('Cont.: ',`e`.`contrario`,'<br/>Abog.: ',`e`.`abogadoContrario`,'<br/>Proc.: ',`e`.`procuradorContrario`) AS `v_datosContrarios`, `e`.`fecha` AS `fecha`, coalesce(`etp`.`numPlantillas`,0) AS `v_numPlantillas`, `e`.`numeroExpediente` AS `numeroExpediente`, `g`.`IdGestor` AS `IdGestor` FROM (((`expediente` `e` left join (select `persona`.`IdPersona` AS `IdPersona`,`persona`.`nombre` AS `nombre` from `persona`) `c` on((`c`.`IdPersona` = `e`.`IdPersona`))) left join (select `gestor`.`IdGestor` AS `IdGestor`,`gestor`.`nombre` AS `nombre` from `gestor`) `g` on((`g`.`IdGestor` = `e`.`IdGestor`))) left join (select `expedientetieneplantilla`.`IdExpediente` AS `IdExpediente`,count(0) AS `numPlantillas` from `expedientetieneplantilla` group by `expedientetieneplantilla`.`IdExpediente`) `etp` on((`etp`.`IdExpediente` = `e`.`IdExpediente`)))  ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura para la vista `vista_factura`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vista_factura`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `vista_factura`  AS SELECT `f`.`IdFacturaCliente` AS `IdFacturaCliente`, `f`.`IdPersona` AS `IdPersona`, `f`.`remesaExportada` AS `remesaExportada`, `f`.`estadoFactura` AS `estadoFactura`, `f`.`fechaCobro` AS `fechaCobro`, `f`.`IdSerie` AS `IdSerie`, `f`.`IdClientePersona` AS `IdClientePersona`, `f`.`IdBanco` AS `IdBanco`, `f`.`numFactura` AS `numFactura`, `f`.`fechaFactura` AS `fechaFactura`, `f`.`actividad` AS `actividad`, `f`.`cuentaContable` AS `cuentaContable`, `f`.`tipoCobro` AS `tipoCobro`, `f`.`iban` AS `iban`, `f`.`fechaVencimiento` AS `fechaVencimiento`, `f`.`observaciones` AS `observaciones`, `f`.`ambito` AS `ambito`, `f`.`tipoOperacion` AS `tipoOperacion`, `f`.`jsonProductos` AS `jsonProductos`, `f`.`importeBruto` AS `importeBruto`, `f`.`irpf` AS `irpf`, `f`.`totalImpuesto` AS `totalImpuesto`, `f`.`totalFactura` AS `totalFactura`, `f`.`ibanRecibo` AS `ibanRecibo`, `s`.`codigo` AS `codigo`, `c`.`nombre` AS `nombre`, `c`.`nif` AS `nif`, `b`.`banco` AS `banco`, `p`.`nombre` AS `nombrePersona`, `f`.`IdFacturaCliente`in (select max(`facturacliente`.`IdFacturaCliente`) from `facturacliente` where (`facturacliente`.`IdPersona` = `f`.`IdPersona`) group by `facturacliente`.`IdSerie` desc) AS `ultimaFactura`, `f`.`editable` AS `editable`, `f`.`rectificativa` AS `rectificativa` FROM ((((`facturacliente` `f` left join `serie` `s` on((`f`.`IdSerie` = `s`.`IdSerie`))) left join `clientepersona` `c` on((`f`.`IdClientePersona` = `c`.`IdClientePersona`))) left join `bancos` `b` on((`f`.`IdBanco` = `b`.`IdBanco`))) left join `persona` `p` on((`p`.`IdPersona` = `f`.`IdPersona`)))  ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura para la vista `vista_facturainterna`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vista_facturainterna`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `vista_facturainterna`  AS SELECT `f`.`IdFacturaInterna` AS `IdFacturaInterna`, `f`.`IdPersona` AS `IdPersona`, `f`.`IdSerie` AS `IdSerie`, `f`.`IdBanco` AS `IdBanco`, `f`.`IdExpediente` AS `IdExpediente`, `f`.`numFactura` AS `numFactura`, `f`.`fechaFactura` AS `fechaFactura`, `f`.`tipoCobro` AS `tipoCobro`, `f`.`iban` AS `iban`, `f`.`fechaVencimiento` AS `fechaVencimiento`, `f`.`observaciones` AS `observaciones`, `f`.`jsonProductos` AS `jsonProductos`, `f`.`importeBruto` AS `importeBruto`, `f`.`totalImpuesto` AS `totalImpuesto`, `f`.`totalPendiente` AS `totalPendiente`, `f`.`totalFactura` AS `totalFactura`, `f`.`editable` AS `editable`, `f`.`rectificativa` AS `rectificativa`, `f`.`ejercicio` AS `ejercicio`, `f`.`estadoFactura` AS `estadoFactura`, `f`.`fechaCobro` AS `fechaCobro`, `f`.`remesaExportada` AS `remesaExportada`, `f`.`numFacturaRectificada` AS `numFacturaRectificada`, `f`.`mailEnviado` AS `mailEnviado`, `f`.`fechaRemesa` AS `fechaRemesa`, `s`.`codigo` AS `codigo`, `b`.`banco` AS `banco`, `p`.`nombre` AS `nombre`, `p`.`nif` AS `nif`, `fr`.`fechaInicio` AS `fechaInicio`, `fr`.`ibanRecibo` AS `ibanRecibo` FROM ((((`facturainterna` `f` left join `serie` `s` on((`f`.`IdSerie` = `s`.`IdSerie`))) left join `bancos` `b` on((`f`.`IdBanco` = `b`.`IdBanco`))) left join `persona` `p` on((`p`.`IdPersona` = `f`.`IdPersona`))) left join `facturainternarecurrente` `fr` on((`fr`.`IdPersona` = `p`.`IdPersona`))) GROUP BY `f`.`IdFacturaInterna``IdFacturaInterna`  ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura para la vista `vista_facturainternarecurrente`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vista_facturainternarecurrente`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `vista_facturainternarecurrente`  AS SELECT `fr`.`IdFacturaInternaRecurrente` AS `IdFacturaInternaRecurrente`, `fr`.`IdPersona` AS `IdPersona`, `fr`.`IdSerie` AS `IdSerie`, `fr`.`IdBanco` AS `IdBanco`, `fr`.`diasVencimiento` AS `diasVencimiento`, `fr`.`observaciones` AS `observaciones`, `fr`.`jsonProductos` AS `jsonProductos`, `fr`.`importeBruto` AS `importeBruto`, `fr`.`totalImpuesto` AS `totalImpuesto`, `fr`.`totalFactura` AS `totalFactura`, `fr`.`fechaUltimaCreacion` AS `fechaUltimaCreacion`, `fr`.`fechaProximaCreacion` AS `fechaProximaCreacion`, `fr`.`tipo` AS `tipo`, `fr`.`numeroDiasRecurrencia` AS `numeroDiasRecurrencia`, `fr`.`diaRecurrencia` AS `diaRecurrencia`, `fr`.`activa` AS `activa`, `fr`.`fechaInicio` AS `fechaInicio`, `fr`.`fechaBaja` AS `fechaBaja`, `fr`.`ibanRecibo` AS `ibanRecibo`, `fr`.`periodicidad` AS `periodicidad`, `p`.`nombre` AS `nombrePersona`, `p`.`mail` AS `mailPersona`, `s`.`codigo` AS `codigoSerie` FROM ((`facturainternarecurrente` `fr` left join `serie` `s` on((`fr`.`IdSerie` = `s`.`IdSerie`))) left join `persona` `p` on((`p`.`IdPersona` = `fr`.`IdPersona`)))  ;

-- Estructura para la vista `vista_gasto`

--
-- Estructura para la vista `vista_persona`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vista_persona`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `vista_persona`  AS SELECT `p`.`IdPersona` AS `IdPersona`, concat('-',`p`.`IdPersona`,'-') AS `v_IdPersona`, concat(`p`.`nombre`,'<br/>',`p`.`nif`) AS `v_nombreNif`, concat(`p`.`mail`,'<br/>',`p`.`telefono1`) AS `v_mailTelefono`, `p`.`tipo` AS `tipo`, `p`.`tarifa` AS `tarifa`, concat(`p`.`cNombre`,'<br/><a href="mailto:',`p`.`cMail`,'">',`p`.`cMail`,'</a><br/>',`p`.`cTelefono`,'<br/>',`p`.`cHorario`) AS `v_datosContacto`, coalesce(`e`.`numExpedientes`,0) AS `v_numExpedientes`, coalesce(`e`.`gestores`,'') AS `v_gestores` FROM (`persona` `p` left join (select `expediente`.`IdPersona` AS `IdPersona`,group_concat(distinct `expediente`.`IdGestor` separator ',') AS `gestores`,count(0) AS `numExpedientes` from `expediente` group by `expediente`.`IdPersona`) `e` on((`e`.`IdPersona` = `p`.`IdPersona`)))  ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura para la vista `vista_solicitudesinternas`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vista_solicitudesinternas`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `vista_solicitudesinternas`  AS SELECT `s`.`IdSolicitudInterna` AS `IdSolicitudInterna`, `s`.`IdPersona` AS `IdPersona`, `s`.`IdGestor` AS `IdGestor`, `s`.`asunto` AS `asunto`, `s`.`consulta` AS `consulta`, `s`.`fechaSolicitud` AS `fechaSolicitud`, `s`.`estado` AS `estado`, `s`.`jsonMensajes` AS `jsonMensajes`, `s`.`categoria` AS `categoria`, `p`.`nombre` AS `nombrePersona`, `g`.`nombre` AS `nombreGestor` FROM ((`solicitudinterna` `s` left join `persona` `p` on((`s`.`IdPersona` = `p`.`IdPersona`))) left join `gestor` `g` on((`s`.`IdGestor` = `g`.`IdGestor`)))  ;
